      function monthToName(monthnum) {
        var monthname = new Array("Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec");
        monthnum = parseInt(monthnum) - 1;
        return monthname[monthnum];

<div class="uk-width-3-4 uk-container-center uk-text-center uk-margin-large-top" style="padding-left:0">
<h2 class="uk-heading-medium home_dom">OUR SERVICES</h2>
<p class="uk-text-large serv-txt">We have extensive experience in delivering services for European Trips, Business
Events and School Trips. We also cater for one-off events such as Weddings, Hen/Stag Parties and Sports Events.</p>
</div>
<div class="uk-width-1-1 uk-margin-top" style="padding-left:0">
<div class="uk-grid">
<div class="uk-width-medium-1-3 uk-text-center uk-row-first">
<div><img src="https://coachscanner.scdn3.secure.raxcdn.com/img/overseas.png" style="width:212px"></div>
<h2 class="uk-margin-bottom-remove">Overseas hire</h2>
<p class="uk-text-large uk-margin-top-remove uk-text-muted serv_text_p">We cater for a number of overseas trips, our
most frequent trips are Snow/Ski Holidays and Conferences. We are one of a few companies who offer a full European
Operating Licensing and adhere to all European Legislations.</p>
</div>
<div class="uk-width-medium-1-3 uk-text-center uk-row-first">
<div class="img_sml_top"><img src="https://coachscanner.scdn3.secure.raxcdn.com/img/corporate.png" style="width:212px"></div>
<h2 class="uk-margin-bottom-remove">Corporate hire</h2>
<p class="uk-text-large uk-margin-top-remove uk-text-muted serv_text_p">We understand the need for a Professional and
Reliable Coach service and this is why businesses continually use us. We will work alongside your Event Manager to
deliver your itinerary, leaving your staff to focus on more important business.</p>
</div>
<div class="uk-width-medium-1-3 uk-text-center uk-row-first">
<div class="img_sml_top"><img src="https://coachscanner.scdn3.secure.raxcdn.com/img/schools.png" style="width:212px"></div>
<h2 class="uk-margin-bottom-remove">Schools</h2>
<p class="uk-text-large uk-margin-top-remove uk-text-muted serv_text_p">Student and School transportation is a key area
of focus for CoachScanner. Our vehicles are fitted with seat belts, foot rests, ABS braking, braking retarders, speed
limiters and adhere to the highest European safety regulations.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<script>
var modal_login = UIkit.modal("#modal-login", {bgclose:false});
var modal_help = UIkit.modal("#modal-help", {bgclose:false});

function init_login_actions(){
    $(".loginmenu").unbind("click");
    $(".loginmenu").click(function(){
        /*show login modal*/
        modal_login.show();
    });
    $("#login_help_show").unbind("click");
    $("#login_help_show").click(function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        modal_login.hide();
        modal_help.show();
    });
    $("#login_contactnum, #login_password").unbind("keypress");
    $("#login_contactnum, #login_password").keypress(function(){
        $("#tradlogin .uk-text-danger span").addClass("uk-hidden");
    });
    $(".login-btn").unbind("click");
    $(".login-btn").click(function(e){
        if ( $("#tradlogin").parsley().isValid() ) {
            $("#tradlogin").parsley().reset();
            e.preventDefault();
            $.post(base_url+'Action/signin',{'phone': $("#login_contactnum").val(), 'passwd': $("#login_password").val()}, function(result){
                if(result != 'false'){
                    sessionStorage.clear();
                    location.reload();
                }else{
                    $("#tradlogin .uk-text-danger span").removeClass("uk-hidden");
                }
            });  
        }
    });
    $(".gohere").unbind("click");
    $(".gohere").click(function(){
        var thishref = $(this).attr("href");
            if (thishref.indexOf("logout") > -1){
                if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined") {
                    sessionStorage.haslogout='1';
                    window.location.href=thishref;
                }
            }else{
                window.location.href=thishref;
            }
    });
    $("#resetemail").unbind("keypress");
    $("#resetemail").keypress(function(){
        $("#resetpw_custom").addClass("uk-hidden");
    });
    $(".resetpw-btn").unbind("click");
    $(".resetpw-btn").click(function(e){

        if ( $("#resetpw").parsley().isValid() ) {
          e.preventDefault();
          $.post(base_url+'Action/getphonesforemail',{'email': $("#resetemail").val()}, function(result){
            result = $.parseJSON(result);
            if(result == "incorrect"){
              $("#resetpw_custom span").html("Please enter a valid email address.").parent().removeClass("uk-hidden");
            }else if(result == false){
              $("#resetpw_custom span").html("It seems like your emails not registered, please gain a quote to create an account").parent().removeClass("uk-hidden");
            }else{
              /*show modal of phone numbers*/
              var reslen = Object.keys(result).length;
              if (reslen == 1){
                /*send password reset email*/
                $("#modal-checker .spin_txt").html("Sending... Please wait.. ");
                UIkit.modal("#modal-checker", {bgclose:false}).show();

                $.post(base_url+"Action/resetpassword", {'email':$("#resetemail").val(), 'mobile': result[0].mobile}, function(rresponse){
                  /*alert the user. close the modal*/
                  /*modal_help.hide();
                  UIkit.modal.alert("An email has been sent with a link to reset your password.");*/
                  UIkit.modal("#modal-checker").hide();
                  UIkit.modal("#modal-emailsent", {bgclose:false}).show();
                    setTimeout(function(){
                      $("#emailyes").attr("src", base_url+"img/green_tick.png");
                    }, 1500);
                });

              }else if (reslen > 1){
                $("#frm_mobilelist").parsley().destroy();
                $("#mobilelist_container div").html("");
                var content = '';
                /*show modal of numbers associated with the email*/
                 $(result).each(function(index, value) {
                  var sel = '';
                  if (index==0){sel=' data-parsley-mincheck="1" data-parsley-error-message="Please choose mobile number" required';}
                  content += '\
                      <input type="radio" name="mobilenum" value="'+value.mobile+'" '+sel+' data-parsley-checkmobile="" /> '+value.mobile+'<br/>';
                 });
                 $("#mobilelist_container div").html(content);
                 $("#frm_mobilelist").parsley();
                 UIkit.modal("#modal-mobiles", {bgclose:false}).show();
              }
              $("#resetpw").parsley().reset();
            }
          });
        }
    });
    $(".resetpwmob-btn").unbind("click");
    $(".resetpwmob-btn").click(function(e){
        if ( $("#frm_mobilelist").parsley().isValid() ) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var mob = '';
            $.when(
                $("input[name='mobilenum']").each(function(index, value){
                    if($(value).is(":checked")){
                        mob = $(value).val();
                    }
                })
            ).done(function(){
                /*send password reset email*/
                 $("#modal-checker .spin_txt").html("Sending... Please wait.. ");
                UIkit.modal("#modal-checker", {bgclose:false}).show();

                $.post(base_url+"Action/resetpassword", {'email':$("#resetemail").val(), 'mobile': mob}, function(rresponse){
                    /*alert the user. close the modal*/
                    /*UIkit.modal("#modal-mobiles", {bgclose:false}).hide();
                    UIkit.modal.alert("An email has been sent with a link to reset your password.");*/
                    UIkit.modal("#modal-checker").hide();
                    UIkit.modal("#modal-emailsent", {bgclose:false}).show();
                    setTimeout(function(){
                      $("#emailyes").attr("src", base_url+"img/green_tick.png");
                    }, 1500);
                });
            });
          
          
        /* $("#modal-mobiles").modal().hide();
        UIkit.modal.alert("The email has been sent with a link to reset your password.");*/
        }
    });
    $("input[name='mobilenum']").unbind("click");
    $("input[name='mobilenum']").click(function(){
        $("#frm_mobilelist").parsley().reset();
    });
}

init_login_actions();
function get_gpudata(){
    var gp_img = base_url+"img/user-alt@2x.png";
        
    $(".profileimg").attr("src", gp_img);
    
    $(".thumbnail.slim-border a img").attr("src",gp_img); 
  }

  get_gpudata();
</script>
